<Text>This review isn't on their store but is on their online website and service on making a purchase.  In addition, I'm also reviewing the products as well......

After purchasing a new truck, I was looking for a good sealant and polish to shine it up.  After doing a lot research, I chose Adam's products and very glad I did.  I purchased the Polish, Clay Bars, and Graphene Spray (Not the concentrate).  The truck has never looked better and it keeps a glare on it even after a solid rain.  The polish and clay bar are self explanatory but the Graphene spray was definitely the prize of the lot.

Application was easy (and I'm not a pro detailer) and I went with the spray in case I made mistakes.  I've even had neighbors stop by to ask what I used on the truck.  After a wash, I do coat it down with the "graphene" detail spray and the shine pops back just like it was freshly polished.  I couldn't be happier with the purchase.

Online purchase was easy and shipping was within 24 hours.  Because they have to use UPS for liquids, shipping time can be a few days but that's no fault of Adam's......

Keep it up and you have a new follower!</Text><Pics>None< /Pics>< resp>

< rating>

< text>
I am absolutely devastated by the way my dog Percy was treated during his 6 night stay at Canine Corral.

I booked holiday travel late, and so our standard boarding facility was booked. Percy is a frequent boarder due to my work travel, and we're pretty low-maintenance when it comes to boarding standards. All I ask is that he's given his meds as appropriate, he gets a decent amount of exercise, and he stays in clean conditions. By all accounts - he was to be treated as such when I booked his stay at Canine Corral.

When I dropped him off (inside the tiny lobby that barely fit the staff member, me, and my dog), they effectively swapped a clipboard for his leash, without giving me an opportunity to say goodbye or to see the crate he'd be staying in.

They further refused to give him his blanket or toy in his crate, so he had nothing that smelled like home.

The webcam nearly never loaded when I attempted to check in on him. The few times I was able to get it to load, I didn't see him, and I rarely saw ANY dogs at play. More often than not, it was just a still image of the outdated, dirty facility.

When I called 4 days into his stay to see why I hadn't seen him at play and if there was an additional fee I could pay to get him more playtime (which I was more than willing to do), they listed out his 3 scheduled playtimes of the day so that I could check in on the webcam: 10:40-11am, 12:40-1pm (note: the camera isn't active during this time), and 2:40-3pm.

That adds ups to 60 total minutes of play, or one hour out of his crate for the entire day. This is beyond unacceptable.

When I picked Percy up this morning, not only was his nose bone-dry and his fur falling out in puffs (he's a mutt - his grooming is typically very low-maintenance), but big patches of fur on his rear were completely matted. In our years of boarding and daycare, this has never happened. This strongly supports my earlier position that he was just sitting in his crate 23 hours out of every day.

Further, their records didn't indicate that I'd prepaid, although I'd handed my credit card over the night I dropped him off. I'm not entirely sure what it was used for.

I now have to make an appointment at the vet to have his matted fur shaved off.

If you love your dog at all, you'll stay far, far away from this place, and you'll warn other dog-parents to do the same.

Canine Corral should be shut down.</text>

Outstanding restaurant!  Our first visit and we plan to go again in the near future.  The food is terrific and the drinks were excellent.  The live Mariachi band was very very good, but a little too loud for dinner time.  They need to turn down the speakers a few clicks. <time>1511404553018<//time><username>MJ</username><user_id>112762912666139674072<//user_id></record></dataset><record>
< review>
I didn't know about this place until I was walking by and saw pictures of ramen on the window. Finally had a chance to check this place out on Thanksgiving Eve. My dinner companion and I were quickly seated around 7:30pm. Menu isn't overwhelming, options of sushi and various ramen broth with light appetizers.

I opted for the tonkotsu miso while my dinner companion went with the black garlic tonkotsu. My tonkotsu miso was pretty standard to most other places. There were definitely lots of flavor, not overly salty with tender pork. The ramen noodles itself were extra fine in texture, yet not soggy. Nothing too out of the ordinary.

I had few bites of the black garlic tonkotsu and in the future, I'd get this instead. The flavor was stronger, in a nice mix sort of way of light garlic, soysauce(?), with a hint of sweet?. It's unique and I haven't tasted anything like this elsewhere. Ingredients inside was standard to everything else in terms of quality and quantity.

2 eggs per bowl and they're brought on the side, you peel them and add to your ramen. My only dislike would be the "extras" you can include for additional charge. My dinner companion added corn (extra $1) that came on the side as well. There were maybe 20 kernels of corn total. After we both put 1/2 in each, we had to go digging for the corn. Not worth the extra $.

Service was good, atmosphere was nice, restroom was clean, I'll probably be back.</review>

You can bet your asada that Chiquita‚Äôs is one of my new favorite restaurants!

Chiquita‚Äôs has been run by Gabriel‚Äôs family for nearly 55 years which shines through in their delicious menu.

Everything was extremely well done but the enchilada and margarita really stood out! We got to try the vegan enchilada and really hope it will get added to the menu! <user_id>117645950927398792687</user_id><user_name>Venus Beckom<//user_name><time>1488123247583</time><Rate>2</Rate>< text>
So I was visiting friends and they asked if I was in the mood for Mexican food...üòêüòí duh! Service was great and the place was very clean! We sat at the bar where the very friendly bartender gave us drink options and promptly provided said drinks-excllently crafted- and took our orders. The food came pretty quickly, which was cool because they were starving. And here is my problem with this place:did you REALLY just charge me $7.05 per taco for "crispy" gr beef tacos so saturated with oil that they were not only completely soft but gave my other food an oil bath containing meat so salty it burned my friggin tongue? Also, why do you think salt, garlic powder and chili powder makes gr beef taco meat??  Plus, if yo are an actual sit-down restaurant too busy to handcraft your re-fried beans, fine but do SOMETHING to make it yours/flavorful- aside from dumping copious amounts of salt into them and topping it with the most generic-non melting cheddar cheese you can find then coupling it with your bland over-cooked rice and charging for the privilege! Also maybe google how to cook Mahi Mahi before you torture this beautiful delicate fish with your heavy-handed cooking methods and serving up a fillet the consistency of Mahi Mahi jerky! Seriously Chiquita's you aught be ashamed of yourself for abusing your loyal local clientele and newcomers with the bait and switch of great service and disgusting food! Hone your craft...google is your friend!</text>
